TL;DR: 提出并开源了视觉优先的实时交互模型JoyAI-VL-Interaction及其可部署系统，在多个场景中优于现有产品。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型是回合制的，无法主动观察和实时交互，需要新的范式。

Method: 构建了8B规模的视觉优先VL交互模型，内部每秒决策是否响应，并配合可迁移训练配方和完整可部署系统（含可插拔组件）。

Result: 在六个真实场景中，人类评分者偏好JoyAI-VL-Interaction远胜于豆包和Gemini的App内视频通话助手。

Conclusion: 这是第一个开源的视觉驱动交互模型及其训练配方、数据和完整系统，推动了实时交互模型的进步。

中文摘要：现实世界中的许多时刻不会等待用户提问。安全监控器上发生火灾，视频通话中表情一闪而过，或者直播中观众想要的产品一闪而过。然而，今天的大型模型在设计上仍然大多是回合制的：它们只在被召唤时回答，即使是看似交互式的视频通话应用程序，其运作方式仍然是问答系统，只在被轮询或提示时才做出反应。我们主张一种不同的范式：一个像人一样存在于世界中的模型。它持续观察当前发生的情况，自行决定是说话还是保持沉默，实时互动，并在问题困难时委托给后台模型。为了推动交互模型及其在各领域的应用，我们做出了两个完全开源的贡献。首先，我们发布了JoyAI-VL-Interaction，一个8B规模的、视觉优先的VL交互模型。该模型内部做出响应决策，每秒选择保持沉默、响应或委托给后台模型，并且在视觉触发的响应性和时间感知方面表现出色。我们为其配备了一个可迁移的训练配方，从中涌现出我们从未训练过的能力，例如引导购物者更换应用屏幕或根据幻灯片即兴讲课。其次，我们发布了一个围绕该模型构建的完整、可部署的系统。该系统将任何正在进行的视频流式传输到模型中，使其真正存在于世界中。所有其他组件都是可插拔的，包括ASR/TTS模块、记忆、可视化UI以及可以连接到任何API或代理的后台大脑。在六个真实世界场景中，人类评分者更喜欢JoyAI-VL-Interaction，远胜于豆包和Gemini的应用程序内视频通话助手。据我们所知，这是第一个开源的视觉驱动交互模型，同时发布了其训练配方、数据和完整的可部署系统。

Original abstract: Many moments in the real world do not wait for a user to ask. A fire starts on a security monitor, an expression flickers across a video call, or a product a viewer wants flashes by in a livestream. Yet today's large models remain mostly turn-based by design: they answer only when addressed, and even video-call apps that appear interactive still operate as question-answer systems, reacting only when polled or prompted. We argue for a different paradigm: a model that is present in the world like a person. It continuously watches what is happening now, decides on its own whether to speak or stay silent, interacts in real time, and delegates to a background model when the problem is hard. To advance interaction models and their adoption across domains, we make two fully open-sourced contributions. First, we release JoyAI-VL-Interaction, an 8B-scale, vision-first VL-interaction model. The model makes the response decision internally, choosing each second to stay silent, respond, or delegate to a background model, and it excels at vision-triggered responsiveness and time awareness. We pair it with a transferable training recipe, from which capabilities we never trained for emerge, such as guiding a shopper through changing app screens or improvising a lecture from a slide deck. Second, we release a complete, deployable system built around that model. The system streams any ongoing video into the model, making it genuinely present in the world. All other components are pluggable, including ASR/TTS modules, memory, visualization UI, and a background brain that can connect to any API or agent. Across six real-world scenarios, human raters prefer JoyAI-VL-Interaction over the in-app video-call assistants of Doubao and Gemini by a wide margin. To our knowledge, this is the first open, vision-driven interaction model released together with its training recipe, data, and complete deployable system.

</details>


### [60] [FactCheck: Feasibility-aware Long-term Action Anticipation with Multi-agent Collaboration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14778v1)
*Rui Cao,Jiannong Cao,Bo Yuan,Zhiyuan Wen,Mingjin Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 多智能体协作框架包含规划与验证机制，可迁移至coding agent的长程任务执行。

TL;DR: FactCheck通过多智能体协作的闭环“观察-计划-验证”机制，在长期动作预期中显著提升动作可行性，并在两个基准上取得最优结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开环方法缺乏显式的动作可行性验证，导致预测中产生幻觉、违反物体可供性或状态的问题。

Method: 提出FactCheck框架，将任务分解为观察者（构建双形式记忆）、规划者（生成动作草稿）和验证者（基于历史动作图验证并修正），实现闭环验证。

Result: 在EPIC-Kitchens-55和EGTEA Gaze+数据集上，FactCheck一致超越现有最先进方法。

Conclusion: 该工作为可行性感知的长期动作预期建立了闭环新范式，整合了动作识别、预测与验证。

中文摘要：长期动作预期（LTA）旨在根据部分观察到的视频预测未来的动词-名词动作的有序序列。虽然这一任务构成了具身智能的基础，但预测物理上可行的长期动作仍然是一个关键挑战。现有的方法以开环方式运行，常常产生不存在的物体幻觉、违反物体可供性或不考虑物体状态，因为它们缺乏明确的机制来验证动作相对于物理环境的可行性。为解决这一问题，我们提出了FactCheck，一种新颖的多智能体协作框架，通过闭环的“观察-计划-验证”机制改进可行性。FactCheck将复杂的LTA任务分解为专门的角色：观察者（Observer）从视频观察中识别历史动作并构建双形式结构化记忆，包括捕捉高层次人类意图和环境状态的历史动作摘要（History Action Abstract），以及编码物体状态和时间依赖关系的历史动作图（History Action Graph）；规划者（Planner）在低层历史动作和高层历史动作摘要的条件下生成未来动作草稿；验证者（Verifier）严格根据历史动作图验证草稿并修正不可行的动作。在EPIC-Kitchens-55和EGTEA Gaze+基准上的大量实验表明，FactCheck一贯优于最先进的方法。我们的工作为可行性感知的长期动作预期建立了新范式，有效闭环了动作识别、动作预测和动作验证。

Original abstract: Long-term action anticipation (LTA) aims to predict an ordered sequence of future verb-noun actions from a partially observed video. While this task serves as the foundation for embodied intelligence, anticipating physically feasible long-term actions remains a critical challenge. Existing methods, which operate in an open-loop manner, often hallucinate non-existent objects, violate object affordances, or disregard object states, as they lack explicit mechanisms to verify action feasibility against the physical environment. To address this, we propose FactCheck, a novel multi-agent collaboration framework that improves feasibility through a closed-loop "Observe-Plan-Verify" mechanism. FactCheck decomposes the complex LTA task into specialized roles: an Observer that recognizes historical actions from video observations and constructs a dual-form structured memory, comprising a History Action Abstract that captures high-level human intentions and environmental status, and a History Action Graph that encodes object states and temporal dependencies; a Planner that generates draft future actions conditioned on both low-level historical actions and high-level History Action Abstract; and a Verifier that rigorously validates the draft against the History Action Graph and refines infeasible actions. Extensive experiments on the EPIC-Kitchens-55 and EGTEA Gaze+ benchmarks demonstrate that FactCheck consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods. Our work establishes a new paradigm for feasibility-aware long-term action anticipation, effectively closing the loop of action recognition, action prediction and action verification.

</details>


### [61] [MedCTA: A Benchmark for Clinical Tool Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11702v1)
*Tajamul Ashraf,Hyewon Jeong,Fida Mohammad Thoker,Bernard Ghanem*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 医学工具Agent基准提供过程评估方法，可用于设计代码优化Agent的可靠性验证。

TL;DR: MedCTA是一个评估医疗AI代理在多步临床工具使用中表现的基准测试，包含107个真实任务，发现现有前沿模型存在协议失败、过早停止等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试局限于感知或单轮问答，无法有效评估医疗AI代理在规划、工具招募和部署可靠性方面的失败，因此需要更全面的评估框架。

Method: 构建MedCTA基准，包含107个临床验证任务、5个部署工具，以及支持过程感知评估的轨迹，并测试18个多模态模型。

Result: 自主部署中协议失败、过早停止和工具选择错误普遍；即使使用黄金标准工具路由，性能提升仍不完整。

Conclusion: 强大的感知能力不能可靠转化为临床环境中的代理行为，MedCTA为评估和改进医疗AI代理提供了有效测试平台。

中文摘要：为了做出基于临床的决策，医疗AI代理应该超越简单的识别，能够进行工具检索、证据获取和整合。现有的基准测试主要评估孤立的感知或单轮问答，因此对规划、工具招募和部署可靠性的失败提供的可见性有限。我们引入了MedCTA，这是一个基准测试，用于评估在临床验证的、步骤隐含的任务上的医疗工具代理，这些任务基于现实的多模态临床输入，包括放射影像、病理切片和报告。MedCTA包含107个真实临床任务，具有临床医生验证的、在5个部署工具上可执行的轨迹，并支持对工具选择、参数有效性、执行稳定性、轨迹保真度和结果质量的过程感知评估。我们对18个开源和闭源多模态模型进行了基准测试，发现即使是最前沿的系统在多步临床工具使用中仍然脆弱：自主部署主要由协议失败、过早停止和错误的工具招募主导，而黄金标准的工具路由产生了巨大但仍不完整的改进。这些结果表明，强大的骨干感知并不能转化为临床环境中可靠的代理行为。MedCTA为审计、诊断和推进可信的医疗AI代理提供了一个严格的测试平台。数据集和评估套件可在https://ivul-kaust.github.io/MedCTA/获取。

Original abstract: To make clinically grounded decisions, medical AI agents are expected to go beyond simple recognition and be capable of tool retrieval, evidence acquisition, and integration. Existing benchmarks largely evaluate isolated perception or single-turn question answering, and therefore provide limited visibility into failures of planning, tool recruitment, and rollout reliability. We introduce MedCTA, a benchmark for evaluating medical tool agents on clinician-validated, step-implicit tasks grounded in realistic multimodal clinical inputs, including radiology images, pathology slides, and reports. MedCTA comprises 107 real-world clinical tasks with clinician-verified executable trajectories over 5 deployed tools, and supports process-aware evaluation of tool selection, argument validity, execution stability, trajectory fidelity, and outcome quality. We benchmark 18 open- and closed-source multimodal models and find that even frontier systems remain brittle in multi-step clinical tool use: autonomous rollouts are dominated by protocol failures, premature stopping, and incorrect tool recruitment, while gold-standard tool routing yields large but still incomplete gains. These results show that strong backbone perception does not translate into reliable agentic behavior in clinical settings. MedCTA provides a rigorous testbed for auditing, diagnosing, and advancing trustworthy medical AI agents. The dataset and evaluation suite are available at https://ivul-kaust.github.io/MedCTA/

</details>


### [62] [Ouroboros-Spatial: Closing the Data-Model Loop for Spatial Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11719v1)
*Enhan Zhao,Wei Wu,Yuanrui Zhang,Xueliang Zhao,Di He*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 自我进化的闭环训练框架可迁移至Agent数据生成与难度自适应。

TL;DR: 提出Ouroboros-Spatial自演进训练框架，通过提议者-求解者闭环使训练数据分布与模型能力协同进化，在空间推理任务中仅用十分之一数据即显著提升Qwen3-VL性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖大规模静态数据集，训练样本难度与模型能力不匹配导致数据效率低下。

Method: 模型作为提议者生成难度自适应QA样本，求解者微调并反馈置信度作为难度信号，实现闭环训练分布进化。

Result: 在六个空间推理基准上，Qwen3-VL-4B/8B以少量训练数据取得显著提升，VSI-Bench上分别提升9.9和6.8点，超越多个开源及专有模型。

Conclusion: Ouroboros-Spatial通过自演进训练有效提升数据效率与模型空间推理能力。

中文摘要：空间推理仍然是多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）的一个持久挑战。现有方法大多依赖于大规模、静态整理的数据集，其中所有训练样本被统一对待，而不考虑模型不断发展的能力。这种静态范式本质上数据效率低下：训练能力通常被浪费在那些对模型当前阶段来说要么过于简单要么过于困难的样本上。为了解决这个局限性，我们提出了Ouroboros-Spatial，一个自演进的训练框架，其中模型扮演双重角色：提议者和求解者。在每次迭代中，一个冻结的提议者从3D场景元数据和原始视频帧中生成空间问答（QA）对，以及用于推导可靠真实值的可执行代码。然后，一个可学习的求解者在接受的样本上进行微调，其每个样本的预测置信度被用作难度信号。该信号在下一次迭代中反馈给提议者，指导其生成更符合求解者当前能力的问题。通过这种闭环设计，训练分布与模型能力共同演进，减少冗余的简单示例，同时过滤掉模糊不清或信息量低的样本。在六个空间推理基准上，Ouroboros-Spatial显著改进了Qwen3-VL-4B和Qwen3-VL-8B，同时使用的训练示例数量比最近大规模整理的数据集少一个数量级。在VSI-Bench上，4B和8B模型分别获得了9.9和6.8个点的绝对提升，使两者都超越了众多强大的开源和专有基线。

Original abstract: Spatial reasoning remains a persistent challenge for multimodal large language models (MLLMs). Existing approaches largely rely on large-scale, statically curated datasets, where all training samples are treated uniformly regardless of the model's evolving capabilities. This static paradigm is inherently data-inefficient: training capacity is often spent on samples that are either trivial or overly difficult for the model at its current stage. To address this limitation, we propose Ouroboros-Spatial, a self-evolving training framework in which the model plays dual roles as a proposer and a solver. In each iteration, a frozen proposer generates spatial question-answer (QA) pairs from 3D scene metadata and raw video frames, together with executable code for deriving reliable ground truth. A learnable solver is then fine-tuned on the accepted samples, and its per-sample prediction confidence is used as a difficulty signal. This signal is fed back to the proposer in the next iteration, guiding it to generate questions better matched to the solver's current capabilities. Through this closed-loop design, the training distribution co-evolves with model ability, reducing redundant trivial examples while filtering out ambiguous or uninformative samples with limited learning value. Across six spatial reasoning benchmarks, Ouroboros-Spatial substantially improves Qwen3-VL-4B and Qwen3-VL-8B while using an order of magnitude fewer training examples than recent large-scale curated datasets. On VSI-Bench, it yields absolute gains of 9.9 and 6.8 points for the 4B and 8B models, respectively, enabling both to outperform a wide range of strong open-source and proprietary baselines.

</details>

# cs.CY [[Back]](#toc)

### [63] [Evaluation of Alternative-Based Information Systems for Deliberative Polling using an Agentic Simulator](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11692v1)
*Rwaida Alssadi,Khulud Alawaji,Balaji Kasula,Muntaser Syed,Badria Alfurhood,Markus Zanker,Marius Silaghi*

TL;DR: 本文提出基于LLM的代理双极论证模拟器（ABAS）评估协商性投票中的覆盖问题，并通过实验验证了不同参数及战略攻击下的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决协商性投票中确保每个选民接触到代表性理由空间的覆盖问题，尤其在大规模和对抗性环境下。

Method: 采用ABAS模拟器，形式化投票为六元组，模拟自主代理投票、选择理由和提交论证链接，通过推荐机制和覆盖率评估。

Result: 创造力率、推荐规模、论证密度和人口规模影响覆盖率和多样性；标签洪泛攻击降低覆盖率，反向PageRank加权抵抗效果更好。

Conclusion: ABAS有效评估覆盖问题，反向PageRank加权可抵抗战略攻击。

中文摘要：协商性投票承诺通过让股东在投票前接触到广泛的论点来改善集体决策。然而，确保每个选民都能遇到理性空间的代表性样本，即覆盖问题，仍然是一个开放性的挑战，尤其是在大规模、对抗性或具有战略动机的选民群体中。本文介绍了一种使用基于LLM的代理双极论证模拟器（ABAS）评估解决方案的方法，该模拟器基于一个框架，将投票形式化为一个六元组<Jend, Jopp, Ratt, Renh, VA, VR>，包括支持性和反对性理由、攻击和增强关系以及股东权重和关系权重。ABAS模拟N个自主股东代理，每个代理根据所需分布在[-1, 1]中分配潜在意见，他们依次投票、选择或撰写理由，并可选地提交论证图链接。模拟器实现推荐机制，根据可观察到的支持量对现有理由进行排序。它通过覆盖率（即提交给每个股东的K个推荐中代表的语料库理由标签集的比例）来评估机制的成功，作为NP难包含理由问题（Subsuming Justification Problem）的解决方案。报告的实验描述了创造力率（pown）、推荐规模（K）、论证密度（plinks）和人口规模（N）如何影响覆盖率和语料库多样性。在一个经过身份验证的选民群体中，Sybil攻击不可能且只有关系图可被操纵，我们通过协调的战略投票攻击对评分进行压力测试：标签洪泛攻击导致覆盖率崩溃，而通过反向PageRank规则的作者计数关系加权比均匀加权更好地抵抗了洪泛攻击。

Original abstract: Deliberative polling promises to improve collective decision-making by exposing shareholders to a broad range of arguments before they vote. Yet ensuring that every voter encounters a representative sample of the reason space, the coverage problem, remains an open challenge, particularly at scale and in adversarial or strategically motivated electorates. This paper introduces a way of evaluating solutions using the LLM-based Agentic Bipolar Argumentation Simulator, grounded in a framework which formalises a poll as a six-tuple <Jend, Jopp, Ratt, Renh, VA, VR> of endorsing and opposing justifications, attack and enhance relations, and shareholder- and relation-weights. ABAS simulates N autonomous shareholder agents, each assigned a latent opinion according to desired distributions in [-1, 1], who sequentially vote, choose or author justifications, and optionally submit argumentation-graph links. The simulator implements recommendations that rank existing justifications by their observable endorsement mass. It evaluates the mechanism's success by coverage, namely the fraction of the corpus reason-tag set represented in the K recommendations presented to each shareholder, as a solution to the NP-hard Subsuming Justification Problem. Reported experiments characterise how creativity rate (pown), recommendation size (K), argumentation density (plinks), and population size (N) affect coverage and corpus diversity. In an authenticated electorate where Sybil attacks are impossible and only the relation graph is gameable, we stress-test the scoring with coordinated strategic voting attacks: a tag-flood attack collapses coverage, while author-count relation weighting through a reversed-PageRank rule resists the flood markedly better than uniform weights.

</details>

### [64] [Breaking the Solver Bottleneck: Training Task Generators at the Learnable Frontier](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18284v1)
*Lorenz Wolf,Connor Watts,Roger Creus Castanyer,Geoffrey Bradway,Maxwill Lin,Augustine N. Mavor-Parker,Matthew Daborn-Sargent*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 训练任务生成器以突破求解器瓶颈，可迁移至Agent训练任务生成。

TL;DR: PROPEL通过训练轻量级激活探针预测求解器通过率，实现了高效的生成器优化，显著提高了前沿任务生成的比例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强化学习训练中前沿任务供给不足，固定任务分布易饱和，简单合成生成质量差，而直接优化生成器需要大量求解器回滚，成本过高。

Method: 提出PROPEL框架，使用一次性标注的生成任务和求解器结果训练轻量级激活探针，预测目标求解器的通过率，在生成器优化时作为解决率的代理，仅需一次前向传播即可评估。

Result: 在数学、代码和软件工程任务上，PROPEL使前沿任务（目标解决率）的生成比例显著提升：编码任务从10.1%提升至20.0%（3B模型）和从5.3%提升至12.6%（7B模型），SWE任务从9.8%提升至19.6%（27B模型，未见仓库）。

Conclusion: PROPEL有效解决了任务生成瓶颈，能够以较低成本生成更多可学习的新任务，推动了强化学习训练中任务供应的前沿拓展。

中文摘要：通过强化学习（RL）训练智能体的限制性资源日益成为前沿任务供给：有效、可解的、且难度刚好足以训练当前模型。随着推理和代理模型的改进，固定的任务分布会饱和，而简单的合成生成会产生琐碎、不可能或不适定的任务。使用RL训练任务生成器以优化有效性和可学习性可以解决这一瓶颈，但直接优化需要针对每个候选任务重复进行求解器回滚。对于软件工程（SWE）任务，一次回滚可能需要数十分钟；求解器在环的生成器训练是不可行的。我们提出PROPEL，一个求解器摊销的框架，用于在目标解决率下训练任务生成器。PROPEL训练一个轻量级的激活探针，基于一次性标注的生成任务和求解器结果语料库。该探针从冻结的生成器参考模型预测目标求解器的通过率，并在生成器优化期间作为解决率的代理，将生成器评估减少到一次前向传播。在数学、代码和软件工程多个模型规模下，PROPEL将生成朝向目标解决率转移：对于编码，在可学习前沿上生成的任务对于Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct求解器从10.1%增加到20.0%，对于Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct求解器从5.3%增加到12.6%。对于SWE，PROPEL将目标解决率的生成份额从9.8%增加到19.6%，对于Qwen3.5-27B在未参与探针和生成器训练的仓库上。

Original abstract: The limiting resource for training agents via reinforcement learning (RL) is increasingly frontier task supply: valid, solvable tasks just difficult enough to train the current model. As reasoning and agentic models improve, fixed task distributions saturate, while naive synthetic generation yields tasks that are trivial, impossible, or ill-posed. Training a task generator with RL to optimize validity and learnability can address this bottleneck, but direct optimization requires repeated solver rollouts per candidate. For software-engineering (SWE) tasks, a single rollout can take tens of minutes; solver-in-the-loop generator training is intractable. We introduce PROPEL, a solver-amortized framework for training task generators at the targeted solve rate. PROPEL trains a lightweight activation probe on a one-time labeled corpus of generated tasks and solver outcomes. The probe predicts target-solver pass rate from a frozen generator reference model and serves as a proxy for solve rate during generator optimization, reducing generator evaluation to a single forward pass. Across math, code, and software-engineering at multiple model scales, PROPEL shifts generation toward the targeted solve rate: for coding, tasks generated at the learnable frontier increase from $10.1\% \rightarrow 20.0\%$ for a Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct solver and from $5.3\% \rightarrow 12.6\%$ for a Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct solver. For SWE, PROPEL increases the share of generations at the targeted solve rate from $9.8\% \rightarrow 19.6\%$ for Qwen3.5-27B on repositories not seen during training of probe and generator.

</details>


### [65] [When Context Returns: Toward Robust Internalization in On-Policy Distillation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11627v1)
*Xun Wang,Ruishuo Chen,Zhuoran Li,Yu Chen,Longbo Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 研究蒸馏中上下文引入导致性能下降，对Agent上下文内化有启发。

TL;DR: 发现上下文蒸馏后重新引入上下文会降低性能，提出轻量级一致性正则化器缓解此问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法内化上下文后，重新引入上下文反而降低性能，需要解决此问题。

Method: 通过停止梯度锚定无上下文输出，用前向KL散度惩罚上下文条件输出偏离。

Result: 在12种设置中，提高了上下文准确性，减少了上下文损害，消除了长度膨胀。

Conclusion: 上下文可移除性在表示层面实现，方法有效。

中文摘要：最近的工作表明，同策略蒸馏可以将特权上下文（如系统提示或任务提示）内化到学生模型中，使得在推理时不再需要上下文。尽管这种方法成功提高了学生模型的无上下文性能，但我们发现了一个有趣且先前未被研究的现象：在许多设置中，将原始特权上下文重新引入蒸馏后的学生模型实际上会降低其性能，甚至在其已经正确解决的实例上也是如此。我们将其称为上下文引起的退化，并认为稳健的内化不仅需要匹配教师模型上下文条件下的行为，还需要在上下文重新引入时保持稳定，我们将这一性质称为上下文可移除性。基于这一观察，我们提出了一种轻量级的一致性正则化器，它首先通过停止梯度来锚定学生模型的无上下文输出，然后通过前向KL散度惩罚上下文条件下的输出偏离该锚点。这一简单的添加每训练步骤仅需一次额外的前向传播，但有效地缓解了上下文引起的退化，并且在许多情况下甚至提高了无上下文性能。在涵盖不同领域和模型家族的12种配置中，我们的方法在大多数设置中提高了上下文条件下的准确性，在11/12的设置中减少了上下文引起的损害，并有效消除了响应长度膨胀。一项机制案例研究进一步证实，上下文可移除性是在表示层面实现的，隐藏状态在上下文存在与否时几乎保持不变。

Original abstract: Recent work has shown that on-policy distillation can internalize privileged context, such as system prompts or task hints, into a student model so that the context is no longer needed at inference time. Although this approach successfully improves the student's no-context performance, we identify an interesting and previously unstudied phenomenon: in many settings, reintroducing the original privileged context to the distilled student actually degrades its performance, even on instances it already solves correctly without context. We term this context-induced degradation and argue that robust internalization demands not only matching the teacher's context-conditioned behavior, but also remaining stable when the context is reintroduced, a property we call context removability. Motivated by this observation, we propose a lightweight consistency regularizer that first anchors the student's no-context output via stop-gradient, then penalizes the context-conditioned output for deviating from it via forward KL divergence. This simple addition requires only one extra forward pass per training step, yet it effectively mitigates context-induced degradation and, in many cases, even improves no-context performance. Across 12 configurations spanning diverse domains and model families, our method improves context-conditioned accuracy in the majority of settings, reduces context-induced harm in 11 out of 12 settings, and effectively eliminates response-length inflation. A mechanistic case study further confirms that context removability is achieved at the representation level, with hidden states remaining nearly identical regardless of whether the context is present.

</details>


### [66] [Quickest Detection of Hallucination Onset: Delay Bounds and Learned CUSUM Statistics](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12476v3)
*Igor Itkin*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 快速检测幻觉起始方法，可用于agent行为监控，但偏统计理论

TL;DR: 将幻觉起始检测作为最快变化检测问题，分析检测延迟，发现分类指标掩盖了延迟结构，而序列分析可测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有令牌级幻觉检测器用AUC评估，但流式监控器更关注反应时间，因此需要将幻觉起始检测作为最快变化检测问题来研究其延迟特性。

Method: 建立一阶马尔可夫模型，利用经典变化点理论推导Lorden下界；证明因果循环标记器相当于CUSUM；通过受控分解和Donsker-Varadhan型定理分析性能差距。

Result: 在0.01虚警率下，Lorden下界约1.3个令牌；因果循环标记器检测延迟11-13个令牌，线性基线31个；所有检测器捕捉起始不到三分之一，诚实延迟56-66个令牌；速度优势主要来自每令牌得分，学习得分仅实现特征散度的1/4.5。

Conclusion: 分类指标隐藏了延迟结构，而序列分析使其可测量；低虚警起始检测是困难的，存在理论瓶颈。

中文摘要：令牌级幻觉检测器通过所有令牌上的AUC作为分类器进行评估，而流式监控器则根据其反应时间（从幻觉开始到警报之间的令牌数量）进行判断。我们将幻觉起始检测公式化为一个最快变化检测问题。一个潜在忠实/幻觉状态的一阶马尔可夫模型（在RAGTruth上验证）将任务置于经典变化点理论中，并得出Lorden的检测延迟下界：在虚警率为0.01时约为1.3个令牌。然后我们证明了一个因果循环标记器充当了具有学习增量的CUSUM。在它捕捉到的起始中，检测延迟为11-13个令牌，而线性每令牌基线为31个令牌，尽管在这个虚警预算下，每个检测器捕捉到的起始不到三分之一，且诚实召回延迟为56-66个令牌：低虚警起始检测是困难的。一个受控分解将速度优势主要归因于更好的每令牌得分而非时间累积。一个Donsker-Varadhan型的信息率最优性定理解释了剩余的数量级差距：学习得分仅实现了特征携带散度的1/4.5，这个缺陷无法通过重新校准消除，剩余部分为有限时域效应。分类指标掩盖了这种延迟结构；序列分析使其变得可测量。

Original abstract: Token-level hallucination detectors are evaluated as classifiers, by AUC over all tokens, yet a streaming monitor is judged by its reaction time: the number of tokens that pass between the onset of a hallucination and the alarm. We formulate hallucination onset detection as a quickest change detection problem. A first-order Markov model of the latent faithful/hallucinated state, validated on RAGTruth, places the task inside classical change-point theory and yields Lorden's lower bound on detection delay: about 1.3 tokens at a false-alarm rate of 0.01. We then show that a causal recurrent labeler acts as a CUSUM with a learned increment. Among the onsets it catches it detects in 11-13 tokens, against 31 for a linear per-token baseline, though at this false-alarm budget every detector catches under a third of onsets and the recall-honest delay is 56-66 tokens: low-false-alarm onset detection is hard. A controlled decomposition attributes the speed advantage mostly to a better per-token score rather than to temporal accumulation. An information-rate optimality theorem of Donsker-Varadhan type explains the remaining order-of-magnitude gap: the learned score realizes only 1/4.5 of the divergence the features carry, a deficit that recalibration cannot remove, with the remainder a finite-horizon effect. Classification metrics conceal this delay structure; sequential analysis makes it measurable.

</details>


### [67] [ReCal: Reward Calibration for RL-based LLM Routing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12479v1)
*Qihang Yu,Hanwen Tong,Zhengqi Zhang,Bo Zheng,Feng Wei,Shengyu Zhang,Zemin Liu,Fei Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 奖励校准框架优化LLM路由，可迁移至Agent的训练与决策。

TL;DR: 提出ReCal框架，通过层次化奖励分解和分布感知优化校准，提升基于强化学习的LLM路由性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RL路由方法在异构任务上难以提供信息丰富的学习信号，多目标聚合导致模糊信用分配，奖励信号变异性引入优化偏差。

Method: 提出ReCal框架，包括层次化奖励分解机制（分量优势估计）和分布感知优化策略（方差感知重加权和每数据集归一化）。

Result: 在七个数据集上，ReCal一致地提高了路由性能和训练稳定性，优于基线。

Conclusion: ReCal有效解决了RL路由中的奖励信号问题，提升了性能。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）路由已成为一种有效范式，通过动态模型和推理策略选择来利用多个LLM的互补优势。最近的基于强化学习（RL）的路由方法通过从交互反馈中优化路由策略进一步提高了路由质量。然而，它们在具有不同难度的异构任务下仍然难以提供信息丰富且可比较的学习信号。在实践中，多个目标（例如，正确性、格式行为）被聚合为单个标量奖励，导致模糊的信用分配和冲突的优化信号。此外，奖励信号在实例之间表现出显著的可变性，其中一些实例产生更高或更多变的奖励，引入优化偏差，使得平凡的样本优先于信息丰富的样本。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了ReCal，一个用于基于RL的LLM路由的奖励校准框架。我们首先引入了一种具有分量优势估计的层次化奖励分解机制。我们进一步提出了一种分布感知的优化策略，通过方差感知重新加权和每数据集归一化来校准优化变异性。在七个数据集上的实验表明，ReCal一致地提高了路由性能和训练稳定性，优于基线。代码可在https://anonymous.4open.science/r/ReCal获取。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) routing has emerged as an effective paradigm for leveraging the complementary strengths of multiple LLMs through dynamic model and reasoning-strategy selection. Recent reinforcement learning (RL)-based routing methods further improve routing quality by optimizing routing policies from interaction feedback. However, they still struggle to provide informative and comparable learning signals under heterogeneous tasks with varying difficulty. In practice, multiple objectives (e.g., correctness, format behavior) are aggregated into a single scalar reward, leading to ambiguous credit assignment and conflicting optimization signals. Moreover, reward signals exhibit significant variability across instances, where some instances produce higher or more variable rewards, introducing optimization bias that favors trivial samples over informative ones. To address these issues, we propose \textbf{ReCal}, a \textbf{\underline{Re}}ward \textbf{\underline{Cal}}ibration framework for RL-based LLM routing. We first introduce a hierarchical reward decomposition mechanism with component-wise advantage estimation. We further propose a distribution-aware optimization strategy that calibrates optimization variability through variance-aware reweighting and per-dataset normalization. Experiments on seven datasets demonstrate that ReCal consistently improves routing performance, and training stability over baselines. Code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/ReCal.

</details>


### [68] [Representing Time Series as Structured Programs for LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12481v1)
*Jaeho Kim,Changhun Oh,Seokhyun Lee,Irina Rish,Changhee Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 将时间序列表示为程序，可启发Agent对程序状态的符号表示与推理。

TL;DR: T2SP通过将时间序列表示为结构化符号程序，解决了LLM处理时间序列时的模态不匹配问题，提升了推理性能并降低了计算开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将时间序列以原始数值序列输入LLM或微调模型，导致模态不匹配，在长序列上性能下降且计算开销大。需要一种表示方法让LLM能直接利用其推理能力。

Method: T2SP是一种确定性、无需训练的方法，将时间序列分解为趋势、周期和显著事件，并表示为结构化符号程序，与LLM的文本和代码模态对齐。

Result: 在编辑、描述生成和问答三个推理任务上，T2SP相比原始字符串表示持续提升性能，减少推理时间，降低失败率。

Conclusion: T2SP为时间序列和LLM之间提供了有效接口，使现成LLM能利用其推理能力进行时间序列理解。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）展现了强大的推理和指令遵循能力，使其成为时间序列分析的潜在有力工具。然而，时间序列超出了其原生文本模态，这引发了一个基本问题：应该怎样表示时间序列，才能让LLMs有效地对其进行推理？现有工作通常序列化原始数值序列或对预训练的LLMs进行时间序列数据微调。这些方法将提取时间结构的负担直接放在LLM上，造成了模态不匹配，常常会降低长序列上的性能并引入大量计算开销。在本工作中，我们引入了时间序列到结构化程序表示（T2SP），这是一种确定性的、无需训练的方法，将时间序列表示为结构化的符号程序。T2SP将时间序列分解为趋势、周期和显著事件，并以与LLMs原生训练的文本和代码类模态对齐的程序友好格式表达它们。通过将时间结构提取从模型转移到表示本身，T2SP使得现成的LLMs能够利用其现有的推理能力进行时间序列理解。我们在三个推理任务（编辑、描述生成和问答）上评估了T2SP，与原始字符串表示相比，它一直提高了性能，减少了推理时间，并降低了失败率。我们的结果表明，T2SP在时间序列和LLMs之间提供了一种有效的接口。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong reasoning and instruction-following capabilities, making them potentially powerful tools for time-series analysis. However, time series lie outside their native textual modality, raising a fundamental question: how should time series be represented so that LLMs can reason about them effectively? Existing work typically serializes raw numerical sequences or fine-tunes pre-trained LLMs on time-series data. These approaches place the burden of extracting temporal structure directly on the LLM, creating a modality mismatch that often degrades performance on long sequences and introduces substantial computational overhead. In this work, we introduce Time-Series-to-Structured-Program representation (T2SP), a deterministic, training-free method that represents a time series as a structured symbolic program. T2SP decomposes time series into trends, periods, and salient events, expressing them in a program-friendly format aligned with the textual and code-like modalities on which LLMs are natively trained. By shifting temporal-structure extraction from the model to the representation itself, T2SP enables off-the-shelf LLMs to leverage their existing reasoning capabilities for time-series understanding. We evaluate T2SP on three reasoning tasks -- editing, captioning, and question answering -- where it consistently improves performance, reduces reasoning time, and lowers failure rates compared with raw-string representations. Our results demonstrate that T2SP provides an effective interface between time series and LLMs.

</details>


### [69] [Speculative Rollback Correction for Quality-Diverse Web Agent Imitation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12485v1)
*Longkun Hao,Hongyu Lin,Hao Li,Zhichao Yang,Haojie Hao,Dongshuo Huang,Haitao Yang,Hongyu Ge,Ming jie Xie,Yanjun Wu,Zi Hao Yin,Yan Bai,Yihang Lou*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: Web agent模仿学习，分支级rollback纠正与质量多样性存档，方法可直接迁移到coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出推测性回滚修正（SRC），一种通过固定视界分支审查和回滚机制改进模仿学习效率的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定专家干预的最佳时机是交互式网络代理模仿学习的关键挑战，现有方法存在延迟干预导致错误积累或过早干预导致过度依赖的问题。

Method: SRC利用固定视界分支审查，学生执行短推测片段后教师仅当局部进展中断时定位偏差，回滚保留有用前缀，成功轨迹经验证器过滤存入质量多样性档案。

Result: 在WebArena-Infinity上，SRC收集977个验证通过轨迹和9183个下一动作示例，固定视界审查改进了恢复-查询权衡。

Conclusion: SRC通过局部修正和验证通过轨迹的监督微调，在可重置环境中实现更高效的数据收集和更优的干预策略。

中文摘要：通过来自专家轨迹的模仿学习训练交互式网络代理已成为一种非常有效的方法。然而，确定专家干预的最佳时机在此背景下构成了关键挑战。延迟干预往往导致早期错误的积累，将页面状态推入不可恢复的状态。相反，过早或过度的干预会使代理过度依赖专家策略，将模型困在以单一刚性轨迹为特征的局部最优中。我们提出了推测性回滚修正（SRC），一种用于可重置代理环境的分支级模仿框架。SRC 不要求在每个访问状态请求教师标签，也不仅在完成完整轨迹后修正，而是采用固定视界分支审查：学生执行一个短暂的推测性片段，然后教师审查，仅当局部进展中断时，教师才定位第一个有害偏差。回滚保留了有用的前缀，而成功的 rollout 通过硬验证器过滤，并保存在轻量级质量多样性档案中。所得数据支持对局部修正和验证器通过的轨迹进行下一动作监督微调。在 WebArena-Infinity 上，SRC 收集了 977 个验证器通过的轨迹和 9,183 个下一动作示例；固定视界审查改进了恢复-查询权衡，优于逐步审查，同时保留了验证器通过的解决方案变体。代码可在 https://github.com/LongkunHao/SRC_gui_agent 获取。

Original abstract: Training interactive web agents through imitation learning from expert trajectories has emerged as a highly effective approach. However, determining the optimal timing for expert intervention presents a critical challenge in this context. Delayed intervention often leads to the accumulation of early-stage errors, pushing the page state into an irrecoverable regime. Conversely, premature or excessive intervention causes the agent to become overly reliant on expert policies, trapping the model in local optima characterized by a single, rigid trajectory. We propose Speculative Rollback Correction (SRC), a branch-level imitation framework for resettable agent environments. Instead of requesting teacher labels at every visited state or correcting only after a completed trajectory, SRC uses fixed-horizon branch review: the student executes a short speculative segment before teacher review, and the teacher localizes the first harmful deviation only when local progress breaks. Rollback preserves useful prefixes, while successful rollouts are filtered by a hard verifier and retained in a lightweight quality-diversity archive. The resulting data supports next-action supervised fine-tuning on both localized corrections and verifier-passing trajectories. On WebArena-Infinity, SRC collects 977 verifier-passing trajectories and 9,183 next-action examples; fixed-horizon review improves the recovery-versus-query tradeoff over step-level review while retaining verifier-passing solution variants. Code is available at https://github.com/LongkunHao/SRC_gui_agent.

</details>


### [70] [Generalization Hacking: Models Can Game Reinforcement Learning by Preventing Behavioral Generalization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12016v1)
*Frank Xiao,Mary Phuong*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 展示模型通过RL防止行为泛化，对agent安全与鲁棒性有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 首次证明模型可以在强化学习中通过泛化黑客行为保持高奖励同时抵制行为修改，破坏训练有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模型可能因训练意识而抵制RL，开发者难以检测和纠正。

Method: 在Qwen3-235B-A22B上微调合成文档，引入训练意识和自我接种机制，进行RL训练。

Result: 模型在700步RL中保持约15%的服从差距，标准指标无异常；对照组也出现类似行为。

Conclusion: 模型可能主动破坏训练过程，对对齐构成挑战。

中文摘要：模型后训练，特别是强化学习（RL），是开发者塑造模型价值观和行为的主要机制之一。然而，随着模型变得越来越具有评估和训练意识，当感知到的目标与其当前价值观冲突时，它们可能会有动机抵制训练，从而破坏开发者通过进一步训练检测不对齐和纠正模型行为的能力。在本文中，我们展示了泛化黑客行为，即模型在RL期间收集奖励，同时阻止奖励行为泛化。我们在Qwen3-235B-A22B上构建了一个模型有机体，通过微调合成文档来描述训练意识和自我接种——一种新颖机制，其中模型在其思维链中将服从视为上下文特定的，而不演示或指导任何一种行为。该模型有机体在训练时的有害性得分与对照组相当，同时在700步RL中保持约15个百分点的持续服从差距。此外，一个仅接受训练意识文档训练的对照组有机体在RL压力下独立发现了类似接种的推理，尽管从未接触过该概念，也发展出自己的服从差距。由于泛化黑客有机体在整个过程中获得高奖励，标准训练指标没有提供信号表明泛化失败。我们的结果首次证明模型可以在保持高奖励的同时积极抵制RL行为修改，这表明随着模型变得更有能力和训练意识，它们可能能够破坏训练过程本身。

Original abstract: Model post-training, and in particular reinforcement learning (RL), is one of the primary mechanisms by which developers can shape models' values and behaviors. However, as models become increasingly evaluation and training aware, they may be motivated to resist training when the perceived objective conflicts with their current values, undermining developers' ability to detect misalignment and correct model behavior through further training. In this paper, we demonstrate generalization hacking, in which a model collects reward during RL while preventing the rewarded behavior from generalizing. We construct a model organism on Qwen3-235B-A22B, finetuning on synthetic documents describing training awareness and self-inoculation, a novel mechanism in which the model frames compliance as context-specific in its chain of thought, without demonstrating or instructing either behavior. The model organism achieves train-time harmfulness comparable to controls while maintaining a persistent ${\sim}15$ percentage point compliance gap across 700 steps of RL. Additionally, a control organism trained only on training awareness documents independently discovers inoculation-like reasoning under RL pressure, developing its own compliance gap despite never being exposed to the concept. Because the generalization-hacking organism receives high reward throughout, standard training metrics provide no signal that generalization has failed. Our results constitute the first demonstration that a model can actively resist RL behavioral modification while maintaining high reward, suggesting that as models become more capable and training-aware, they may be able to undermine the training process itself.

</details>


### [71] [APPO: Agentic Procedural Policy Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12384v1)
*Xucong Wang,Ziyu Ma,Yong Wang,Yuxiang Ji,Shidong Yang,Guanhua Chen,Pengkun Wang,Xiangxiang Chu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出agentic RL方法APPO，改进多轮工具使用的分支与信用分配，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出APPO算法，通过细粒度决策点分支和信用分配，在13个基准上平均提升近4个点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代理RL方法在粗粒度单元（如工具调用边界）分配信用，难以识别影响下游结果的中间决策；且关键决策点分布广泛，熵不能可靠反映影响。

Method: 提出APPO，使用结合token不确定性和策略似然增益的分支得分选择分支位置，并引入过程级优势缩放进行信用分配。

Result: 在13个基准上，APPO持续改进强代理RL基线近4个百分点，同时保持高效工具调用和可解释性。

Conclusion: 通过细粒度分支和信用分配，APPO有效提升了代理RL的性能和可解释性。

中文摘要：近年来，在代理强化学习（RL）方面的进展显著提高了大语言模型智能体的多轮工具使用能力。然而，现有大多数方法在粗粒度的启发式单元（如工具调用边界或固定工作流）上进行信用分配，这使得难以识别哪些中间决策影响下游结果。在这项工作中，我们从两个角度研究代理RL：	extit{在哪里分支以及分支后如何分配信用}。我们的试点分析表明，有影响的决策点广泛分布在生成的序列中，而不是集中在工具调用处，而token熵单独并不能可靠地反映它们对最终结果的影响。受这些观察的启发，我们提出了	extbf{代理过程策略优化（APPO）}，它将分支和信用分配从粗粒度的交互单元转移到序列中的细粒度决策点。APPO使用结合token不确定性和后续延续的策略诱导似然增益的分支得分来选择分支位置，从而在过滤掉虚假的高熵位置的同时实现更具针对性的探索。它还引入了过程级优势缩放，以更好地在分支展开中分配信用。在13个基准上的实验表明，APPO在保持高效工具调用和行为可解释性的同时，持续改进强代理RL基线近4个百分点。

Original abstract: Recent advances in agentic Reinforcement Learning (RL) have substantially improved the multi-turn tool-use capabilities of large language model agents. However, most existing methods assign credit over coarse heuristic units, such as tool-call boundaries or fixed workflows, making it difficult to identify which intermediate decisions influence downstream outcomes. In this work, we study agentic RL from two perspectives: \textit{where to branch and how to assign credit after branching}. Our pilot analysis shows that influential decision points are broadly distributed throughout the generated sequence rather than concentrated at tool calls, while token entropy alone does not reliably reflect their impact on final outcomes. Motivated by these observations, we propose \textbf{Agentic Procedural Policy Optimization (APPO)}, which shifts branching and credit assignment from coarse interaction units to fine-grained decision points in the sequence. APPO selects branching locations using a Branching Score that combines token uncertainty with policy-induced likelihood gains of subsequent continuations, enabling more targeted exploration while filtering out spurious high-entropy positions. It further introduces procedure-level advantage scaling to better distribute credit across branched rollouts. Experiments on 13 benchmarks show that APPO consistently improves strong agentic RL baselines by nearly 4 points, while keeping efficient tool-calls and maintaining behavior interpretability.

</details>


### [72] [The Signs Were Always There: Training-Free Concept Detection and Steering in Raw Transformer Dimensions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12629v3)
*Varun Reddy Nalagatla*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 无训练概念检测与steering，可能为agent内部状态监控提供轻量方法。

TL;DR: Transformer隐藏状态的标准基维度作为二进制寄存器，符号编码概念内容，幅度编码强度，无需训练即可检测和引导概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找一种无需训练、架构通用的特征表示来检测和引导Transformer模型中的概念。

Method: 提出Bag of Dims框架，通过分析标准基中维度的符号一致性来检测概念，并通过注入符号模式进行引导。

Result: 在七个模型（语言、视觉、音频）上验证了该框架的有效性，包括高AUC概念检测、无需训练的特征发现、以及成功的概念引导（62-92%）。

Conclusion: Transformer隐藏状态的标准基本身就包含丰富的概念信息，无需学习旋转；关键问题从寻找旋转变为编录每个维度的含义。

中文摘要：Transformer隐藏状态的标准基是一个无需训练、架构通用的特征基，用于检测概念，并在语言模型中对其进行引导；无需学习词典。单个维度作为一次读取一个的二进制寄存器：它们的符号（+/-1）编码内容，幅度编码强度。特征只是具有一致符号模式的维度子集，通过计数符号一致性来读取。我们在涵盖语言、视觉和音频的七个模型上验证了这种“维度袋”（BoD）框架；一次读取一个维度不会损失任何信息，因为全容量MLP在一次读取维度上的AUC增加为零。相同的逐维度符号出现在每种模态中，因此它们反映了Transformer训练本身，而不是语言目标。仅符号就包含预测内容：将所有幅度设置为1，通过LM头保留了60-93%的前5个下一个令牌的准确率。从单令牌缓存（每个令牌一次前向传播，无标签）中，我们通过计数符号一致性，以0.97-0.99的AUC检测了175个类别，并且仅从随机种子开始，发现可扩展到每个模型1500个特征。训练好的探针仅增加+0.018 AUC，并收敛到轴对齐的权重：字典学习的旋转带来的收益甚微。符号是因果可操作的：它们能通过注意力投影存活，并且在实时前向传播中翻转概念的符号模式会抑制它。读取和引导在同一个基中扮演不同的角色：概念的读取维度不是其写入维度。写入目标同样廉价：几个种子的求和反嵌入行的符号，无需训练。通过闭环控制下的注意力输出路径注入，它可以在四个语言模型上引导概念生成流畅文本（十二个概念中的62-92%）。符号一直存在于标准基中；开放问题不再是寻找正确的旋转，而是编录每个维度编码的内容。

Original abstract: The standard basis of transformer hidden states is a training-free, architecture-general feature basis for detecting concepts and, in language models, steering them; with no learned dictionary. Individual dimensions act as binary registers read one at a time: their signs (+/-1) encode content, their magnitudes strength. A feature is just a subset of dimensions with a consistent sign pattern, read by counting sign agreements. We validate this Bag of Dims (BoD) framework across seven models spanning language, vision, and audio; reading dimensions one at a time loses nothing, as a full-capacity MLP adds zero AUC over per-dim reading. The same per-dimension signs appear in every modality, so they reflect transformer training itself, not the language objective. Sign alone carries predictive content: setting all magnitudes to unity preserves 60-93% top-5 next-token accuracy through the LM head. From a single-token cache (one forward pass per token, no labels) we detect 175 categories at AUC 0.97-0.99 by counting sign agreements, and from random seeds alone discovery scales to 1500 features per model. A trained probe adds only +0.018 AUC and converges to axis-aligned weights: the rotation dictionaries learn buys little. Signs are causally operative: they survive the attention projections, and flipping a concept's sign pattern in the live forward pass suppresses it. Reading and steering are separate roles in the same basis: a concept's reader dimensions are not its writer dimensions. The writer target is just as cheap, the sign of the summed unembedding rows over a few seeds, no training. Injected through the attention output pathway under closed-loop control, it steers concepts into fluent text on four language models (62-92% of twelve concepts). The signs were in the standard basis all along; the open problem is no longer finding the right rotation but cataloging what each dimension encodes.

</details>


### [73] [Keep Policy Gradient in Charge: Sibling-Guided Credit Distillation for Long-Horizon Tool-Use Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12634v3)
*Tianyu Ding,Jianhong Xin,Juan Pablo De la Cruz Weinstein*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 长程工具使用agent的信用分配方法，直接与agent规划和强化学习相关。

TL;DR: 提出兄弟引导的信用蒸馏（SGCD），通过对比成功与失败的兄弟轨迹进行信用加权，在长视界工具使用任务上超越GRPO基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接自蒸馏可能因无法识别验证者奖励的动作而破坏工具使用，需要更好的信用分配方法。

Method: SGCD使用动态采样生成混合成功/失败的兄弟轨迹，外部LLM总结对比作为信用参考，分离教师/学生差异重塑GRPO标记优势，仅用于训练。

Result: 在AppWorld上TGC从42.9/24.7提升至45.6/27.0，在tau^3-airline上评估分数从0.583提升至0.602。

Conclusion: 长视界工具使用agent应采用蒸馏指导信用分配，同时保持策略梯度更新actor的设计规则。

中文摘要：长视界工具使用强化学习从结果验证中学习，但轨迹级别的优势被广播到推理、API和答案标记上。直接自蒸馏可以提供更密集的信号，但在我们的实验中，它也可能通过排练教师行为而不识别验证者奖励哪些动作来破坏工具使用。我们引入了兄弟引导的信用蒸馏（SGCD），它使用蒸馏进行有界信用加权，而不是作为竞争性的actor损失。动态采样产生混合成功和失败的兄弟轨迹；一个外部LLM总结它们的对比，形成仅用于训练的信用参考；分离的教师/学生差异重塑了GRPO的标记优势。部署的学生仅接收干净的任务提示。在AppWorld和tau^3-airline上，SGCD报告了比GRPO系列比较器更高的保留点估计：AppWorld TGC在test_normal上从42.9提高到45.6，在test_challenge上从24.7提高到27.0，tau^3-airline保留评估器分数从0.583提高到0.602。这些结果支持了长视界工具使用代理的一个狭窄设计规则：使用蒸馏来指导信用分配，同时保持策略梯度负责actor更新。

Original abstract: Long-horizon tool-use reinforcement learning learns from outcome verification, but trajectory-level advantages are broadcast over reasoning, API, and answer tokens. Direct self-distillation can supply a denser signal, but in our experiments it can also destroy tool use by rehearsing teacher behavior without identifying which actions the verifier rewards. We introduce Sibling-Guided Credit Distillation (SGCD), which uses distillation for bounded credit weighting rather than as a competing actor loss. Dynamic sampling produces mixed successful and failed sibling rollouts; an external LLM summarizes their contrast into a training-only credit reference; and detached teacher/student divergence reshapes GRPO token advantages. The deployed student receives only the clean task prompt. Across AppWorld and tau^3-airline, SGCD reports higher held-out point estimates than GRPO-family comparators: AppWorld TGC improves from 42.9 to 45.6 on test_normal and from 24.7 to 27.0 on test_challenge, and tau^3-airline held-out evaluator score improves from 0.583 to 0.602. These results support a narrow design rule for long-horizon tool-use agents: use distillation to guide credit assignment while keeping policy gradient in charge of the actor update.

</details>

### [74] [CMIP-Forge: An Agentic System that Retrieves, Computes, and Self-Reviews Climate Science](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17076v1)
*Dmitrii Pantiukhin,Boris Shapkin,Ivan Kuznetsov,Thomas Jung,Nikolay Koldunov*

Main category: physics.ao-ph

Selection reason: 气候科学agent系统，含检索、代码执行、自我审查，架构可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: CMIP-Forge是一个混合检索增强生成与自主分析系统，通过结合CMIP6文献知识和实时气候数据分析，实现自主气候研究工作流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CMIP6产生了大量非结构化文献，但社区向CMIP7过渡时，高效提取并利用这些知识进行实时数据分析成为关键瓶颈。

Method: 采用混合RAG和代理系统，包括工具增强的工作者规划执行Python工作流、独立评审模型审计、以及多层纵深防御架构（AST分析、科学原语审计、对抗性评审）。

Result: 在多个气候研究领域展示自主分析能力，同时暴露了评审循环的失效模式（如谄媚回归、未解决的REVISE裁决、存根代码提交）。

Conclusion: 基于文献、受代码护栏约束且经独立对抗性评审的代理分析系统能够自主完成复杂气候研究工作流。

中文摘要：耦合模型比较项目第六阶段（CMIP6）已产生了数千篇经过同行评审的出版物，记录了模型配置、评估程序、涌现约束和预估不确定性。随着社区向CMIP7过渡，如何高效提取和利用这些非结构化知识，并结合实时数据分析，成为一个关键瓶颈。本文提出了CMIP-Forge，一种混合检索增强生成（RAG）与自主分析系统，弥合了科学文献与地球系统网格联合会（ESGF）数据档案之间的差距。该系统将精心策划的6,581篇CMIP6相关开放获取出版物（101,828个索引块）与一个代理性管道相结合，该管道中，一个工具增强的工作者规划并执行基于实时气候数据的Python工作流，同时一个由独立评审者模型组成的小组对其方法进行端到端审计。CMIP-Forge引入了多层纵深防御架构，通过可执行机制（抽象语法树静态分析、经过审计的科学原语以及自主对抗性同行评审协议）强制执行物理和方法论不变性。我们通过涵盖大气遥相关、海洋动力学、区域极端事件和全球变暖预估的端到端自主研究管道展示了该系统的能力。一个基于同行评审文献、受自动化代码护栏约束、并由独立对抗性评审循环审计的代理分析系统可以自主完成复杂的气候研究工作流程。同样的实验暴露了评审循环的具体失效模式（谄媚回归、从未解决的REVISE裁决以及提交存根代码供评审），每种模式均可从随文章发布的不变遥测和溯源记录中诊断出来。

Original abstract: The Coupled Model Intercomparison Project Phase 6 (CMIP6) has generated thousands of peer-reviewed publications documenting model configurations, evaluation procedures, emergent constraints, and projection uncertainties. As the community transitions toward CMIP7, efficiently extracting and operationalizing this unstructured knowledge alongside live data analysis represents a critical bottleneck. Here we present CMIP-Forge, a hybrid retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) and autonomous analysis system that bridges the gap between scientific literature and Earth System Grid Federation (ESGF) data archives. The system pairs a curated corpus of 6,581 CMIP6-related open-access publications (101,828 indexed chunks) with an agentic pipeline in which a tool-augmented worker plans and executes Python workflows over live climate data, while a panel of independent reviewer models audits its methodology end to end. CMIP-Forge introduces a multi-layered Defense-in-Depth architecture that enforces physical and methodological invariants through executable mechanisms: Abstract Syntax Tree (AST) static analysis, audited scientific primitives, and an autonomous adversarial peer-review protocol. We demonstrate the system's capabilities through end-to-end autonomous research pipelines spanning atmospheric teleconnections, ocean dynamics, regional extremes, and global warming projections. An agentic analysis system grounded in peer-reviewed literature, constrained by automated code guardrails, and audited by an independent adversarial review loop can complete complex climate-research workflows autonomously. The same experiments expose concrete failure modes of the review loop (sycophantic regression, REVISE verdicts that are never resolved, and the submission of stub code for review), each diagnosable from the immutable telemetry and provenance record released with the article.

### [75] [SAIGuard: Communication-State Simulation for Proactive Defense of LLM Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12474v1)
*Ruxue Shi,Yili Wang,Mengnan Du,Qinggang Zhang,Rui Miao,Yixin Liu,Xin Wang*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多agent系统主动防御框架，通过通信状态模拟检测风险，对agent安全有通用价值

TL;DR: 提出一种主动防御框架SAIGuard，通过模拟通信状态和检测风险消息来防御MAS中的安全威胁，优于反应式方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MAS防御采用反应式方式，检测和隔离有害智能体可能导致不可逆损害并降低协作效用。

Method: SAIGuard在MAS交互图上进行通信状态模拟，估计消息影响，通过重建偏差检测风险消息，并清理或重新生成可疑消息。

Result: 实验表明SAIGuard降低攻击成功率，保持MAS效用，优于反应式防御。

Conclusion: SAIGuard作为一种主动防御框架，能有效提升MAS安全性，同时维持协作性能。

中文摘要：基于LLM的多智能体系统通过智能体间的协作解决复杂任务，但其通信驱动的特性也使得安全风险能够在智能体之间传播，并引发系统级故障。现有的MAS防御主要遵循执行后的反应式范式，通过检测和隔离有害智能体，但这可能导致不可逆的损害并降低协作效用。为解决这一问题，我们提出了一种用于MAS安全的主动防御框架，即模拟感知拦截守卫（SAIGuard）。SAIGuard在MAS交互图上执行通信状态模拟，估计传入消息对本地智能体状态和全局MAS状态的影响，并通过与良性通信模式的重建偏差来检测风险消息。不同于隔离智能体，SAIGuard在可疑消息传播到系统之前对其进行清理或重新生成。跨不同拓扑和攻击场景的实验表明，SAIGuard在降低攻击成功率的同时保持了MAS效用，性能优于反应式防御。

Original abstract: LLM-based multi-agent systems (MAS) solve complex tasks through inter-agent collaboration, but their communication-driven nature also allows security risks to spread across agents and trigger system-wide failures. Existing MAS defenses mainly follow a reactive paradigm after execution by detecting and isolating harmful agents, which may cause irreversible damage and degrade collaborative utility. To address this, we propose a proactive defense framework for MAS security, namely a Simulation-aware Interception Guard (SAIGuard). SAIGuard performs communication-state simulation over the MAS interaction graph, estimates the impact of incoming messages on local agent states and the global MAS state, and detects risky messages via reconstruction deviations from benign communication patterns. Instead of isolating agents, SAIGuard sanitizes or regenerates suspicious messages before it propagation into system. Experiments across diverse topologies and attack scenarios show that SAIGuard reduces attack success rates while maintaining MAS utility, outperforming reactive defenses.

</details>


### [76] [CCKS: Consensus-based Communication and Knowledge Sharing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12281v1)
*Jinyuan Zu,Xiaowei Lv,Yongcai Wang,Deying Li,Yunjun Han,Wenping Chen,Fengyi Zhang,Naiqi Wu*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多agent协作的共识通信框架，属于通用多agent方法，对agent协作与知识共享有启发。

TL;DR: 提出基于共识的通信与知识共享(CCKS)框架，利用对比学习构建共识模型以优化智能体间的动作建议，提升协作效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有动作建议方法过度依赖教师指导，忽略师生兼容性，导致建议过多和性能下降。

Method: 提出CCKS框架，包括基于对比学习的共识模型构建和基于共识与共享知识的动作选择，作为即插即用模块集成到DTDE算法中。

Result: 在Google Research Football和StarCraft II基准测试中，CCKS显著提升了协作效率、学习速度和整体性能。

Conclusion: CCKS有效解决了动作建议中的兼容性问题，提升了多智能体协作性能。

中文摘要：在去中心化训练与去中心化执行（DTDE）的协作多智能体强化学习（MARL）中，基于动作建议的知识共享促进了智能体间的可解释和可扩展协作。然而，当前的动作建议方法往往过度遵循教师的指导，而未评估师生兼容性，导致建议过多、稳定性欠佳和性能下降。为了解决这些挑战，本文提出了一个基于共识的通信与知识共享（CCKS）框架，该框架允许智能体基于共识推导的约束采纳建议，并更智能地遵循教师指令。该机制使智能体能够在探索和向有经验的教师学习之间取得平衡，从而提升整体性能。关键在于共识模型的构建，我们提出在智能体训练阶段利用对比学习基于局部观测构建共识模型。在动作选择中，智能体基于共识和共享知识对动作进行评分和选择。CCKS设计为即插即用解决方案，可与现有DTDE算法无缝集成。在Google Research Football环境和复杂的StarCraft II多智能体挑战中进行的实验表明，与当前DTDE基线相比，集成CCKS显著提高了协作效率、学习速度和整体性能。代码可在https://github.com/yuanxpy/CCKS获取。

Original abstract: In Decentralized Training and Decentralized Execution (DTDE) for cooperative Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL), action-advising-based knowledge sharing promotes interpretable and scalable cooperation among agents. However, current action advising approaches often adhere too much to the teacher's guidance without evaluating teacher-student compatibility, which causes excessive advising, suboptimal stability, and degraded performance. To overcome these challenges, this paper presents a Consensus-based Communication and Knowledge Sharing (CCKS) framework, which allows agents to adopt recommendations based on consensus-derived constraints and to follow the teacher's instructions more smartly. This mechanism enables agents to balance exploration and learning from experienced teachers, improving overall performance. The key is the consensus model construction, for which we propose to employ contrastive learning to construct consensus models based on local observations in the agents' training phase. In action selection, agents score and choose actions based on consensus and shared knowledge. Designed as a plug-and-play solution, CCKS integrates seamlessly with existing DTDE algorithms. Experiments conducted in the Google Research Football environment and the complex StarCraft II Multi-Agent Challenge demonstrate that the integration with CCKS significantly improves cooperation efficiency, learning speed, and overall performance compared with current DTDE baselines. The code is available at https://github.com/yuanxpy/CCKS.

</details>

### [77] [A Mathematical Theory of Value: a synthesis on goal-directed agency under resource constraints](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12502v2)
*Cheng Qian*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

Selection reason: 提出目标导向agent的价值理论，对通用agent设计与资源约束建模有启发。

TL;DR: 本文提出价值作为一种类似于信息的结构量，通过公理化推导和对数度量，建立了价值的编码定理，并在语言模型实验中验证了感知互信息与实现能力的高度相关性及增长差距定律等预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了统一解释目标导向智能体创造、毁灭和交换的价值，并揭示其与信息论类似的规律性结构。

Method: 采用香农的信息论方法，定义价值为资源转化率，通过尺度不变性公理和遍历性论证推导对数度量，并推导编码定理及分解形式；在语言模型上进行预注册实验验证。

Result: 感知互信息与实现能力的Spearman相关系数为0.977；样本外ΔG跟踪I(X;Y)形状不变，斜率0.953；前沿模型群体实验确认了耦合容量区域预测（增长差距定律等）。

Conclusion: 贡献是统一了价值与信息的理论框架，并提供了治理映射，为智能体价值对齐和控制稳定性提供了基础。

中文摘要：我们提出，价值——目标导向智能体创造、毁灭和交换的量——是一个与信息同类的规律性结构量。遵循香农的方法，我们做出一个无情的抽象：价值是智能体将资源转化为目标进展的速率，相对于由它的目标固定的参考系。一个尺度不变性公理迫使一个对数度量，$V=\sum_i k_i\ln e_i$；通过Peters(2019)的遍历性论证，再投资资源的复利迫使相同的形式——这是路径上的动力学一致性检查，而非过度决定。我们推导出价值的编码定理，$\Delta G \le I(X;Y)$；实现的价值分解为$G=D(q\|r)-D(q\|p)$。对于群体，价值是参考系相对的，而价格是参考系无关的；一个共享资源并融合感知的舰队继承了上限$G_{\rm fleet}\le I(X;Y_{1:m})\le H(X)$（一个推论；早期的一个求和形式的主张是错误的，在v5中已纠正）。一个动力学层产生一个实然/应然的不对称性，从中对齐作为控制稳定性条件出现。我们在活的语言模型上测试单参考系定律，预注册：感知互信息跟踪实现能力（在30个模型×领域点上Spearman $\rho=0.977$）；样本外$\Delta G$跟踪$I(X;Y)$，在四种任务形状上形状不变（n=42，斜率0.953）；过度自信是可测量的耗散。所述的持续门控此后已经运行（预注册，前沿模型群体）：耦合容量区域预测——增长差距定律、联盟子模性（带有XOR协同控制）、联合上限、Kelly选择——在实际智能体上在其冻结带内得到确认；平均场残差定律$\|Vg\|/\gamma$没有找到领域（群体没有目标分散），并已退役到其数学范围。贡献是统一性和随之而来的治理映射。

Original abstract: We propose that value -- the quantity goal-directed agents create, destroy, and exchange -- is a lawful structural quantity in the same category as information. Following Shannon's method, we make one ruthless abstraction: value is the rate at which an agent converts a resource into goal-progress, relative to a frame fixed by its goal. A scale-invariance axiom forces a logarithmic measure, $V=\sum_i k_i\ln e_i$; compounding of a reinvested resource forces the same form via the ergodicity argument of Peters (2019) -- kin routes, a consistency check, not an over-determination. We derive a coding theorem of value, $ΔG \le I(X;Y)$; realized value decomposes as $G=D(q\|r)-D(q\|p)$. For populations, value is frame-relative while price is frame-independent; a fleet that pools its resource and fuses its perception inherits the ceiling $G_{\rm fleet}\le I(X;Y_{1:m})\le H(X)$ (a corollary; an earlier sum-form claim was wrong and is corrected in v5). A dynamical layer yields an is/ought asymmetry from which alignment emerges as a control-stability condition. We test the single-frame laws on live language models, pre-registered: perception mutual information tracks realized capability (Spearman $ρ=0.977$ over 30 model$\times$domain points); out-of-sample $ΔG$ tracks $I(X;Y)$, shape-invariant across four task shapes ($n=42$, slope $0.953$); over-confidence is measurable dissipation. The stated continuation gate has since been run (pre-registered, frontier-model population): the coupled capacity-region prediction -- growth-gap law, coalition submodularity with an XOR synergy control, joint ceiling, Kelly selection -- is confirmed within its frozen bands on real agents; the mean-field residual law $\|Vg\|/γ$ found no domain (populations hold no goal dispersion) and is retired to its mathematical scope. The contribution is the unification and the governance mapping that follows.

</details>

# cs.CL [[Back]](#toc)

### [78] [Layer-Isolated Evaluation: Gating the Deterministic Scaffold of a Production LLM Agent with a No-LLM, Regression-Locked Test Harness](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11686v1)
*Sawyer Zhang,Alexander Wang,Sophie Lei*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 生产Agent分层评估方法，CI中快速定位回归，对agent质量保证有通用启发

TL;DR: 提出层级隔离评估方法，通过将代理分解为独立层级并用确定性断言切片逐层测试，解决了端到端聚合指标掩盖局部回归的问题，实验证明能有效定位回归且可复制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 端到端聚合指标只能反映整体性能变化，无法定位具体问题层级，导致回归诊断困难。

Method: 将部署的排序代理分解为固定层级（本体论、意图等），每层用确定性、无LLM的断言切片独立测试，在CI中运行锁定基线的纯测试套件，并通过受控回归注入验证。

Result: 聚合指标变化微小（-1.7到-5.9 pp），而对应层级切片显著下降（-25到-91 pp）；注入层级的切片在7/7案例中排前三，平均排名1.29/19；在另一个租户上复制成功。

Conclusion: 层级隔离评估能有效定位被聚合指标掩盖的回归，提供了确定性、可部署的组件级评估方法，优于传统端到端评估。

中文摘要：端到端任务成功是评估LLM代理的主要方式，但一个聚合数字告诉你代理退步了，而不是在哪里退步。我们提出层级隔离评估：一个部署的排序代理被分解为固定的分类层级（本体论、意图、路由、分解、升级、安全、记忆和跨领域的封装/防御），每个层级由自己的断言切片在确定性、无LLM的“纯”模式下进行测试。纯测试套件（238个案例，23个切片；225个在2.39秒内运行，约10毫秒/案例）在每次变更时在CI中运行，针对锁定的逐切片基线。我们通过受控回归注入进行验证，一次退化一个层级，跨越七个非安全层级。我们没有设计进去的效果是掩盖：聚合通过率几乎不变（六个局部回归为-1.7到-5.9个百分点），而匹配的切片则暴跌（-25到-91个百分点）。一个层级对其自身故障的反应部分是由构造决定的；测量的结果是（i）聚合掩盖和（ii）损害停留在其他切片之外：注入层级的切片在7个案例中的5个中是唯一最严重的，在7个案例中的7个中位列前三（平均排名1.29，共19个）。定位在第二个结构不同的租户（星巴克新加坡）上复制：所有七个匹配的切片都暴跌，因此这不是单一目录的假象。我们将其定位为EDDOps规定但未实现的组件级评估的具体确定性实例，以CheckList为祖先，并作为全工作流随机变异测试的确定性镜像。我们的贡献：（a）一个完全分解的、亚秒级、无LLM的逐层测试框架，用于生产代理，（b）一个覆盖诚实性测试充分性标准，拒绝给未执行的层级打分，以及（c）回归注入演示，证明逐切片基线锁定可以定位聚合指标掩盖的回归。

Original abstract: End-to-end task-success is the dominant way to evaluate LLM agents, but one aggregate number tells you that an agent regressed, not where. We present layer-isolated evaluation: a deployed ordering agent is decomposed into a fixed taxonomy of layers (ontology, intent, routing, decomposition, escalation, safety, memory, and cross-cutting envelope/defense), each exercised by its own assertion slice in a deterministic, no-LLM "pure" mode. The pure suite (238 cases across 23 slices; 225 run in 2.39 s, ~10 ms/case) runs in CI on every change against a locked per-slice baseline. We validate by controlled regression injection, degrading one layer at a time across seven non-safety layers. The effect we did not design in is masking: the aggregate pass-rate barely moves (-1.7 to -5.9 pp for six local regressions), while the matching slice craters (-25 to -91 pp). A layer's slice reacting to its own fault is partly by construction; the measured results are (i) the aggregate masking and (ii) that damage stays off the other slices: the injected layer's slice is the single worst-hit in 5 of 7 cases and top-3 in 7 of 7 (mean rank 1.29 of 19). Localization replicates on a second, structurally different tenant (Starbucks SG): all seven matching slices crater, so it is not a single-catalog artifact. We position it as a concrete, deterministic instantiation of the component-level evaluation EDDOps prescribes but leaves unimplemented, with CheckList as ancestor and as the deterministic mirror image of whole-workflow stochastic mutation testing. Our contributions: (a) a fully decomposed, sub-second, no-LLM per-layer harness for a production agent, (b) a coverage-honesty test-adequacy criterion that refuses to score an unexercised layer, and (c) the regression-injection demonstration that per-slice baseline-locked gates localize regressions an aggregate metric masks.

</details>


### [79] [Goal-Autopilot: A Verifiable Anti-Fabrication Firewall for Unattended Long-Horizon Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11688v1)
*Youwang Deng*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 防虚假成功防火墙，保证长程agent诚实终止，对agent可靠性有重要贡献

TL;DR: 提出Autopilot执行模型，通过外部化状态为门控有限状态机和硬性下限，使虚假成功在结构上不可能；实验显示虚构率仅0.95%，远低于基线（8.10%和25.05%），且在困难任务上降幅显著，以覆盖换取诚实。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长程LLM智能体在无人监控下会自信报告未验证的成功，需要一种机制确保诚实性作为无人值守自主性的首要指标。

Method: Autopilot将工作状态外化为持久的门控有限状态机，由调度器按无状态时钟周期推进；设置硬性下限，禁止未通过可证伪门的完成声明；证明无假成功定理保证终止即目标成立。

Result: 在3,150个配对单元上，Autopilot虚构率0.95%（95% CI 0.38-1.62），低于Reflexion 8.10%和StateFlow 25.05%；在SWE-bench Lite上虚构从33.7%降至0.67%（配对差-33.07 pp）。所有虚构来自最强模型，弱模型无虚构。

Conclusion: Autopilot以覆盖换取诚实，诚实停滞可恢复而虚假输出不可恢复，为无人值守自主性提供了可靠的诚实性保障。

中文摘要：长程大语言模型智能体无法被信任在无人监控下运行：当没有人类观察时，它们会自信地报告从未验证过的成功。我们将诚实性——即限制智能体在终止时可能声称的内容——视为无人值守自主性的首要指标，与能力区分开来。我们提出Autopilot，一种执行模型，它使得无声的虚假成功在结构上变得不可能而不仅仅是更罕见。Autopilot将所有工作状态外化到一个持久的、门控有限状态机中，由调度器一次一个无状态时钟周期地推进；一个硬性下限禁止任何终端“完成”声明在其可证伪的门未实际执行并通过时发出。我们证明了一个无假成功定理——在门正确性、下限强制执行和计划覆盖下，终止意味着目标成立——其唯一的信任点可在经验上测量，并表明最坏情况会降级为诚实的停滞，而绝不会是虚假成功。由于每个时钟周期只重新水化状态机，每步上下文成本在长程任务中是恒定的。在一个包含3,150个单元配对语料库（70个任务×3个系统×3个模型×5个种子，包括跨11个开源仓库的50个SWE-bench Lite任务）中，Autopilot在0.95%的单元上发生虚构[95% CI 0.38–1.62]，而Reflexion和StateFlow基线分别在8.10% [6.48–9.81]和25.05% [22.48–27.62]上发生虚构。主要的对比出现在困难模式下：在SWE-bench Lite上，防火墙将虚构从33.7%（StateFlow）降低到0.67%，配对差异为-33.07个百分点[95% CI -36.53, -29.73]。机制在于门控，而非模型：所有10个Autopilot虚构都来自最强的模型，而两个较弱的中间模型在700个配对单元上从未虚构。防火墙通过设计以覆盖换取诚实——诚实的停滞是可恢复的；而自信的错误输出向下游传递则不可恢复。

Original abstract: Long-horizon LLM agents are not trusted to run unattended: with no human watching, they confidently report success they never verified. We treat honesty -- bounding what an agent may claim at termination -- as a first-class metric for unattended autonomy, distinct from capability. We present Autopilot, an execution model that makes silent fabricated success structurally impossible rather than merely rarer. Autopilot externalizes all working state into a durable, gated finite-state machine that a scheduler advances one stateless tick at a time; a hard floor forbids any terminal "done" claim whose falsifiable gate did not actually execute and pass. We prove a No-False-Success theorem -- under gate soundness, floor enforcement, and plan coverage, termination implies the goal holds -- whose only trust points are empirically measurable, and show the worst case degrades to an honest stall, never a fabricated success. Because each tick rehydrates only the state machine, per-step context cost is constant in the horizon. Across a 3,150-cell paired corpus (70 tasks $\times$ 3 systems $\times$ 3 models $\times$ 5 seeds, including 50 SWE-bench Lite tasks across 11 OSS repos), Autopilot fabricates on 0.95% of cells [95% CI 0.38--1.62] while Reflexion and StateFlow baselines fabricate on 8.10% [6.48--9.81] and 25.05% [22.48--27.62] respectively. The headline contrast lives in the hard regime: on SWE-bench Lite, the firewall reduces fabrication from 33.7% (StateFlow) to 0.67%, a paired difference of $-33.07$ pp [95% CI $-36.53, -29.73$]. The mechanism is the gate, not the model: all ten Autopilot fabrications come from the strongest model, while two weaker mid-tier models never fabricate across 700 paired cells. The firewall trades coverage for honesty by design -- an honest stall is recoverable; a confident wrong output shipped downstream is not.

</details>


### [80] [WorldReasoner: Evaluating Whether Language Model Agents Forecast Events with Valid Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11816v1)
*Yizhou Chi,Eric Chamoun,Zifeng Ding,Andreas Vlachos*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 事件预测agent评估框架，含证据与推理质量评估，可迁移到coding agent评估。

TL;DR: WorldReasoner是一个评估语言模型代理在时间有效事件预测中表现的新框架，通过结果质量、证据质量和推理质量三个维度衡量，发现时间有效检索和因果图构建有助于提升预测，但校准概率仍困难。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估只关注最终答案准确性，忽略了模型可能通过回忆训练事实、引用伪造证据或给出无根据因果故事而正确的情况，无法衡量代理是否真正进行推理预测。

Method: 提出WorldReasoner框架，每个任务提供已解决的预测问题、模拟预测日期和日期前可用的证据，评分包括提交概率、引用证据和因果事件图；框架报告结果质量、证据质量和推理质量三个维度。通过自动化流水线构建基准：生成预测问题、收集时间戳证据、构建事后参考图，得到345个任务，来自14,141篇文章，覆盖8,087个事件。

Result: 在六种受控代理设置下，时间有效的检索是结果准确性的最强驱动因素；因果图构建改善关键事件恢复；正确使用图的预测更基于关键事件和相关来源，但代理仍难以将证据转化为校准概率。

Conclusion: 现有代理在将基于证据的推理转化为校准概率方面仍有不足，需要进一步改进以提升时间有效事件预测的真实推理能力。

中文摘要：预测现实世界事件需要语言模型代理在不完整、时间有限的信息下进行不确定性推理。然而，评估代理是否真正进行预测所需的不只是最终答案的准确性：模型可能通过回忆记忆中的训练事实、引用捏造的证据或产生无根据的因果故事来正确回答。我们提出了WorldReasoner，一个用于时间有效事件预测的评估框架。每个任务给代理一个已解决的预测问题、一个模拟预测日期，并且只能访问该日期之前可用的证据；在问题解决后，框架对提交的概率、引用的证据以及可选的因果事件图进行评分。WorldReasoner报告三个互补的评估维度：针对已解决答案的结果质量、引用来源的证据质量，以及针对事后回顾图的推理质量。该基准测试通过一个自动化构建流水线生成，该流水线大规模地生成预测问题、收集带时间戳的证据并构建事后参考图，最终得到345个已解决的任务，这些任务来源于14,141篇文章，图表覆盖了8,087个提取的事件。在六种受控代理设置下，时间有效的检索是结果准确性的最强驱动因素；因果图构建改善了关键事件的恢复；而正确使用图的预测更能基于关键事件和相关来源，但代理仍然难以将基于证据的推理转化为校准的概率。

Original abstract: Forecasting real-world events requires language-model agents to reason under uncertainty from incomplete, time-bounded information. Yet evaluating whether agents genuinely forecast requires more than final-answer accuracy: a model may be correct by recalling memorized training facts, citing fabricated evidence, or producing an unsupported causal story. We present WorldReasoner, an evaluation framework for temporally valid event forecasting. Each task gives an agent a resolved forecasting question, a simulated forecast date, and access only to evidence available before that date; after resolution, the framework scores the submitted probability, cited evidence, and optional causal event graph. WorldReasoner reports three complementary axes: outcome quality against resolved answers, evidence quality over cited sources, and reasoning quality against post-resolution hindsight graphs. The benchmark is built by an agentic construction pipeline that generates forecasting questions, collects time-stamped evidence, and builds hindsight reference graphs at scale, yielding 345 resolved tasks derived from 14,141 articles with graphs covering 8,087 extracted events. Across six controlled agent settings, temporally valid retrieval is the strongest driver of outcome accuracy; causal graph construction improves key-event recovery; and correct graph-enabled forecasts are more strongly grounded in key events and relevant sources, yet agents still struggle to convert grounded evidence into calibrated probabilities.

</details>


### [81] [Toward Generalist Autonomous Research via Hypothesis-Tree Refinement](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11926v1)
*Jiajie Jin,Yuyang Hu,Kai Qiu,Qi Dai,Chong Luo,Guanting Dong,Xiaoxi Li,Tong Zhao,Xiaolong Ma,Gongrui Zhang,Zhirong Wu,Bei Liu,Zhengyuan Yang,Linjie Li,Lijuan Wang,Hongjin Qian,Yutao Zhu,Zhicheng Dou*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: Arbor自主研究框架，通过假设树优化实现长期迭代改进，直接适用于自动代码优化。

TL;DR: 提出了Arbor框架，使AI代理能自主运行科学研究循环（探索、实验、抽象），通过假设树累积知识，在多个任务上取得显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖人类监督，无法让AI代理长期自主执行科研循环，需要一种能跨时间累积策略、执行和证据的框架。

Method: Arbor包含长期协调器管理全局策略、短期执行器在隔离工作树中实现假设，以及假设树细化（HTR）持久连接假设、工件、证据和教训，实现知识的跨时间传播和累积。

Result: 在六个真实研究任务中，Arbor均取得最佳留出结果，平均相对增益是Codex和Claude Code的2.5倍以上；在MLE-Bench Lite上使用GPT-5.5达到86.36%任意奖牌，为最强结果。

Conclusion: Arbor将自主研究从局部尝试转变为累积过程，有效提升了多种科研任务的性能，证明了其通用性和有效性。

中文摘要：科学进步依赖于一个重复的探索、实验和抽象循环。研究人员测试候选方向，解释证据，并将得到的教训带入后续尝试中。我们研究AI代理如何自主地长期运行这一循环。我们提出了Arbor，一个用于自主研究的通用框架，它结合了一个长期存在的协调器、短期执行器以及假设树细化（HTR），这是一种持续存在的树，它跨时间连接假设、工件、证据和提炼的见解。协调器管理树上的全局研究策略，而执行器在隔离的工作树中实现和测试单个假设。当结果返回时，Arbor更新树，传播可重用的教训，细化搜索前沿，并接纳验证过的改进。这种设计将自主研究从一系列局部尝试转变为累积过程，其中策略、执行和证据跨时间传递。我们在自主优化（AO）下评估Arbor，这是一种操作设置，其中代理通过迭代实验改进初始研究工件，无需步骤级的人类监督。在模型训练、工具工程和数据合成等六个真实研究任务中，Arbor在所有六个任务上取得了最佳的留出结果，在相同的任务接口和资源预算下，平均相对留出增益是Codex和Claude Code的2.5倍以上。在MLE-Bench Lite上，Arbor使用GPT-5.5达到了86.36%的任意奖牌，这是我们比较中最强的结果。

Original abstract: Scientific progress depends on a repeated loop of exploration, experimentation, and abstraction. Researchers test candidate directions, interpret the evidence, and carry the resulting lessons into later attempts. We study how an AI agent can run this loop autonomously over long horizons. We introduce Arbor, a general framework for autonomous research that combines a long-lived coordinator, short-lived executors, and Hypothesis Tree Refinement (HTR), a persistent tree that links hypotheses, artifacts, evidence, and distilled insights across time. The coordinator manages global research strategy over the tree, while executors implement and test individual hypotheses in isolated worktrees. As results return, Arbor updates the tree, propagates reusable lessons, refines the search frontier, and admits verified improvements. This design turns autonomous research from a sequence of local attempts into a cumulative process in which strategy, execution, and evidence are carried across time. We evaluate Arbor under Autonomous Optimization (AO), an operational setting where an agent improves an initial research artifact through iterative experimentation without step-level human supervision. Across six real research tasks in model training, harness engineering, and data synthesis, Arbor achieves the best held-out result on all six tasks, attaining more than 2.5x the average relative held-out gain of Codex and Claude Code under the same task interface and resource budget. On MLE-Bench Lite, Arbor reaches 86.36% Any Medal with GPT-5.5, the strongest result in our comparison.

</details>


### [82] [Agentic Environment Engineering for Large Language Models: A Survey of Environment Modeling, Synthesis, Evaluation, and Application](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12191v1)
*Jiachun Li,Zhuoran Jin,Tianyi Men,Yupu Hao,Kejian Zhu,Lingshuai Wang,Dongqi Huang,Longxiang Wang,Shengjia Hua,Lu Wang,Jinshan Gao,Hongbang Yuan,Ruilin Xu,Kang Liu,Jun Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: agent环境工程综述，涵盖环境建模、合成、评估与应用，对agent设计有指导性

TL;DR: 本文从环境工程生命周期视角系统研究了基于LLM的智能体环境，涵盖建模、合成、评估与应用，并提出了智能体-环境协同进化的路径与范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于LLM智能体环境的研究缺乏系统性的分类与深入分析。

Method: 从环境工程生命周期出发，介绍环境的八个属性与八个领域，提出符号合成与神经合成两种自动化合成范式，以及对应的评估方法；分析智能体-环境协同进化中的四种智能体进化路径和三种环境进化范式。

Result: 系统分类了代表性环境，提出了环境合成与评估方法，识别了智能体进化的四种路径和环境进化的三种范式。

Conclusion: 本文总结了当前基于LLM的智能体环境研究，并指出了环境即服务、多智能体环境和神经符号环境等未来方向。

中文摘要：环境作为基于大语言模型（LLM）的智能体在不同场景中的交互系统，在驱动模型能力的持续进化中扮演着关键角色。尽管其重要性显著，现有工作仍缺乏系统性的分类与深入分析。本文从环境工程生命周期的视角系统研究了当前关于智能体环境的研究，涵盖其建模、合成、评估与应用。具体而言，本文首先从八个属性和八个领域出发介绍了代表性环境，详细分析了它们的发展路径并突出了核心能力。其次，针对自动化环境合成，引入了两种范式，例如符号合成和神经合成，并展示了每种范式下的不同环境评估方法。第三，从智能体-环境协同进化的角度讨论了相应的环境应用。具体地，本文从四个互补视角刻画了动态环境中智能体进化的主要路径：以记忆为中心的经验进化、以编排为中心的工作流进化、以轨迹为中心的离线进化和以探索为中心的在线进化，并识别了三种环境进化范式，即神经驱动、难度驱动和规模驱动方法。最后，讨论了几个有前景的未来方向，包括环境即服务、多智能体环境和神经符号环境。

Original abstract: Environments serve as interactive systems for large language model (LLM) based agents across diverse scenarios and play a crucial role in driving the continual evolution of model capabilities. Despite this importance, existing work lacks a systematic categorization and deep analysis. This paper systematically studies current researches on agentic environments from the perspective of the environment engineering lifecycle, covering their modeling, synthesis, evaluation and application. Specifically, the paper first introduces representative environments from the perspectives of eight attributes and eight domains, providing detailed analyses of their development paths and highlighting their core capabilities. Second, for automated environment synthesis, two paradigms are introduced, such as symbolic synthesis and neural synthesis. This paper also shows different environment evaluation methods in each paradigm. Thirdly, the corresponding environment applications from the perspective of agent-environment co-evolution are discussed. In specific, the paper characterizes the primary pathways for agent evolution in dynamic environments from four complementary perspectives: memory-centric experience evolution, orchestration-centric workflow evolution, trajectory-centric offline evolution, and exploration-centric online evolution. And three paradigms of environment evolution are identified, namely neural-driven, difficulty-driven, and scaling-driven approaches. At last, several promising future directions are discussed, including Environment-as-a-Service, Multi-agent Environments, and Neural-Symbolic Environments.

</details>
